Southeast

Statistics of the Total Amount of Likin in Five Southeastern Provinces 43

Based on the investigation conducted by the Likin Reduction Committee after the Likin Reduction Conference of the Five Southeastern Provinces in the seventeenth year, the statistics on the total amount of likin in the five provinces and the total amount of special consumption taxes levied, as well as the differences, are very detailed and are recorded separately as follows:

▲ Jiangsu: Tea over 29,400 yuan, cocoons and silk over 1,198,800 yuan, timber over 343,734 yuan, porcelain and pottery over 91,800 yuan, paper over 208,000 yuan, oil over 259,000 yuan, tin foil 170,000 yuan, seafood over 40,000 yuan, livestock over 420,000 yuan, medicinal materials over 48,000 yuan, furs over 19,200 yuan, lacquer over 2,300 yuan, soybeans over 95,000 yuan, cotton over 425,000 yuan, totaling 9 million yuan. The total annual amount of consumption tax levied is approximately 3,357,000 yuan.

The difference compared to likin is a shortfall of over 5,640,000 yuan.

▲ Zhejiang: Tea 240,000 yuan, sugar 255,000 yuan, cocoons and silk 1.9 million yuan, timber 250,000 yuan, paper 300,000 yuan, oil 200,000 yuan, cotton 250,000 yuan, yarn 38,000 yuan, foreign cloth, wool, and down 360,000 yuan, artificial silk 85,000 yuan.

▲ Anhui: Tea 450,000 yuan, sugar 400,000 yuan, cocoons and silk 70,000 yuan, chicken and duck eggs 40,000 yuan, incense powder 5,000 yuan, mining tax 35,000 yuan, others 600,000 yuan, totaling 3.06 million yuan. The total revenue from special taxes levied is 1.16 million yuan, with a difference of 2 million yuan.

▲ Fujian: Tea over 3,290,000 taels, mining tax 2,122,052 taels, timber 596,833 taels, porcelain and pottery 5,918 taels, paper 155,957 taels, oil 17,382 taels, tin foil 150,288 taels, seafood 103,556 taels, medicinal materials 77,506 taels, furs 23,815 taels, totaling 5.13 million yuan.

The total amount of special revenue levied is over 3.3 million yuan, with a difference of over 1.82 million yuan.

▲ Jiangxi: Timber 800,000 yuan, porcelain and pottery 800,000 yuan, ramie cloth 560,000 yuan, paper 500,000 yuan, imported goods over 700,000 yuan, totaling 3.6 million yuan. The total revenue from special consumption taxes levied is 3.2 million yuan, with a difference of 400,000 yuan.

The total likin revenue of the five provinces is 27.89 million yuan, and the total special tax revenue is 15.98 million yuan, with a difference of over 11.9 million yuan. Detailed investigations of other provinces are not yet available.

Hubei Provincial Government Allocates Huge Sum for Dyke Repair 44

▲ The province's dykes and embankments are divided into twenty sections

A dispatch from Hankou reports that the river water has risen early this summer and its momentum is very strong, which is rare in recent years. According to Fang Dazhi, Director of the Yongli Bureau of the Provincial Government, the current situation of active flood prevention is roughly as follows: "Currently, it is the summer flood season and the river water has risen sharply. After dispatching personnel to investigate, the Fankou Dyke sluice gate was found to be dilapidated due to years of disrepair and was breached by the water. The Bureau immediately allocated tens of thousands of yuan to the Dyke Engineering Bureau and ordered them to repair it day and night within a limited time to prevent further collapse. In addition, it was heard that the Sunjia Guai people's dyke in Jinjiang was dug open by the communists, causing the river water to rush in, but no formal report has been received. Personnel have been dispatched to investigate. Whether the river dyke works in the province are solid is of great importance to the people's livelihood. In the past, due to the lack of organization in the employment of dyke workers, malpractices developed and turned into opportunities for corruption and unscrupulous elements to make money. Now, personnel have been sent to repair each dyke. There is no time for further changes. Before the completion of the repair period, many are still unfinished. Therefore, the flood prevention work for this year has been carried out in advance to provide relief. The province's dykes and embankments have been divided into twenty sections, each section is equipped with a flood prevention director who is responsible for paying attention to the dangers and properly arranging protection. At the same time, the previous repair projects will be inspected and reported truthfully, and estimates will be made for the planned repair projects and the required project costs. Based on the past practice of the province sending special commissioners to survey and estimate, the flood prevention funds for this year have also been approved by the provincial government to be allocated 150,000 yuan for application. If it is insufficient in the future, it shall be submitted for additional requests based on the facts. All of the flood prevention directors employed this year are selected from graduates of engineering schools who have rich dyke construction experience to eliminate the dyke worms. Perhaps the accumulated malpractices of the past can be completely eradicated." In addition, Fang issued a circular attached below to stress this year's flood prevention work. [The case follows the Jiangxiang various main dykes. The flood prevention work for this year has been planned into sections and flood prevention directors have been assigned separately. They should immediately lead all levels of staff to the site to carry out the work within a time limit. All of the planning and protection matters should be fully responsible by the directors of each section. It is especially important to rely on the full cooperation and diligent work of all staff to ensure safety. Moreover, the river water has risen early this year and many dyke works are still unfinished. Detailed inspections, attention to dangers, and proper protection are all necessary. It is now found that most of the flood prevention personnel in various places have reported to their posts in compliance with the order, but there are still many who are watching and delaying in the province. They are ignoring their duties and are very unworthy of their appointments. In addition to ordering them separately, the director should immediately follow the investigation and report any staff members who have not reported to their posts before the 10th of this month to be dismissed and replaced. Do not conceal anything. This order is of utmost importance.] (6th)

Wuhan

The Executive Headquarters Strictly Handles the Yuchuan Steamer Earth Case 45

▲ The review committee announced the end of the review

▲ Shen Gong, Director of the Special Tax Office of Hubei and Hunan, has been dismissed

A dispatch from Hankou reports that the Wuhan Garrison Headquarters cracked the Yuchuan Steamer Earth case worth three

Page 8

million yuan. The Executive Headquarters Director He Yingqin advocated strict handling and ordered the Executive Headquarters Aide-de-Camp and Military Law Departments, the Hubei Provincial Government, the Wuhan Garrison Headquarters, the Hubei Finance Special Commissioner's Office, and the Special Tax Supervision Committee to organize a review committee to conduct a strict review. The committee was established on June 14 and has held five review meetings and two temporary meetings, collecting evidence very seriously. When the Xiang Incident occurred, Director He went to Hunan to supervise the troops. He recently sent a telegram from Hunan to Hankou ordering the confiscation of the smuggled earth and ordering the review committee to expedite the review and conclude it. The Executive Headquarters received the telegram and convened various departments to organize a sales committee to conduct a public auction. The review committee held a joint meeting on the 5th and decided to conclude the case as soon as possible, roughly within a week. The main criminals in this case are active-duty soldiers Yang Xiaoxuan and Liu Fuqing. When the Yuchuan Steamer arrived in Hankou, they fled by steamer. Shen Gong Lishi, the Director of the Special Tax Office of Hubei and Hunan, who was suspected of malfeasance, was also dismissed by the Hubei Finance Special Commissioner's Office, and representatives of the Special Tax Office, Zhang Ziqin and Ma Zhaolong, were prepared to be interrogated by the review committee. The original 316 boxes of earth are still being kept under seal by officers designated by the Wuhan Garrison Headquarters. According to Ye Peng, Chief of Staff of the Garrison Headquarters, Commander Xia Douyin had repeatedly ordered a strict investigation of soldiers harboring private smuggling of opium. After this case was cracked, Commander Xia was extremely angry and immediately reported to the Executive Headquarters for legal action. He was subsequently ordered to properly preserve the smuggled earth and send personnel to participate in the review committee. In addition, the Garrison Headquarters did not interfere. The review committee is responsible and someone will be able to fairly handle the matter in the shortest possible time. The Garrison Headquarters is responsible for maintaining the public order in Wuhan and has the duty to strictly investigate soldiers harboring private smuggling of earth. It will continue to fulfill its duties and strictly investigate and arrest those involved so that no one escapes. (July 6)

Chen Guohui's Wanted Order Revoked 46

▲ Fang Shengtao Arrives in Xiamen with Plans for the Fujian Situation

A dispatch from Xiamen reports that Hui was originally a bandit army. When it entered Fujian, it was incorporated into the newly compiled army and then transferred to Longyan to be reorganized into the First Mixed Brigade of the Provincial Defense Army. Last year, the provincial government felt that the incorporated army had not changed its old ways and decided to thoroughly suppress it. Gu Chen's was the most powerful bandit team with ties to outside forces. At that time, the Provincial Chairman Yang Shuzhuang personally came to Xiamen to supervise the suppression of Chen in Tong'an. Chen escaped with his troops to Anxi and occupied Anxi, Yongchun, and Nan'an. The provincial government then reported to the National Government and ordered the arrest of Chen and dozens of others including Ye Dingguo. The provincial committee Lin Zhiyuan supervised the education regiment and repeatedly suppressed them, but failed due to the treacherous mountain roads. Before long, the Fujian situation changed and the military suppression of bandits in southern Fujian completely stopped. Chen supplemented his strength in the Anyong area and became stronger. Recently, the provincial government approved the request of the Fujianese fellow villagers in Shanghai and telegraphed the central government to revoke the wanted order. The National Government has approved it and the provincial government ordered the order to be forwarded to all places. [The National Government Civil Affairs Office telegraphed the order. According to the Fujian Provincial Government's telegram, the Fujianese fellow villagers association in Shanghai stated that Chen Guohui's brigade has been stationed in Anxi, Nan'an, Yongchun and other counties for several months since being pursued by your government and has been able to protect the local people. Recently, they have received messages from various townships stating that since the provincial changes, communist bandits in southern Fujian have taken the opportunity to rise up and people are in great fear. Fortunately, Chen's brigade has been suppressing them and can temporarily alleviate the current situation. However, they fear that if there is no proper solution, the local people will be in an unbearable situation if a change occurs. After careful consideration, the members of the association have earnestly requested your government to approve the revocation of the arrest warrant for the former brigade commander Chen Guohui and Chief of Staff Hong Wende, restore their original positions to test their future achievements and reassure the people. The local future will be greatly benefited and the provincial situation can also be slightly improved. It is reported that bandits and communists are rampant in southern Fujian. The telegram states that Chen Guohui and others, who were born in southern Fujian, should be able to protect the local people. It is proposed to revoke the arrest warrant for Chen Guohui and Hong Wende to give them a chance to rehabilitate themselves and contribute to the Fujian situation. Please investigate and follow the instructions. It is ordered that the order be followed and distributed to all subordinates to inform them of this order.

After the National Government issued the order, Fang Shengtao arrived in Xiamen from Shanghai on June 27. Hong Wende came with him. According to Hong, Chen's revocation of the wanted order and restoration to his original position means his troops now have 4,000 soldiers. It is also said that Fang's arrival in Xiamen was prompted by Fujian Chairman Yang Shuzhuang and various important figures in the central government to clean up the Fujian situation. Fang plans to first eliminate Lu Xingbang in northern Fujian. A brigade will be drawn from the newly compiled division, and all six battalions of the training corps, about 2,600 to 2,700 people, will be combined with Chen Guohui's troops and led by Fang from Yongchun through Dehua to attack Youxi from the side. Youxi is the base of Lu's troops. After Youxi is captured, Yanping will also not be able to hold. Combined with Liu Heding's frontal attack, it will not be difficult to eliminate Lu in one fell swoop. Zhang Zhen has arrived in Xiamen from Zhangzhou on the 29th to meet with Fang and discuss strategy. (4th)

The First Annual Meeting of the Education Society 48

The Chinese Children's Education Society will hold a meeting in Wuxi today to study elementary education, early childhood education, and family education. The society held its inaugural meeting in Hangzhou West Lake in July last year and currently has more than 20 group members and more than 300 individual members. It publishes a monthly journal on children's education. The first annual meeting this summer vacation was held last night by the executive committee. Today, various groups and individuals are arriving one after another. The society has specially contracted the Wuxi Railway Hotel for members to stay. The opening ceremony will be held at Meiyuan at 9:00 this morning. Various agencies in Wuxi are planning to send representatives to the meeting and give speeches, including Dong Renjian, professor of Guanghua University, on the child-centered education movement, Shang Zhongyi, professor of Central University, on the current trends in elementary education, and Hu Shuyi, a member, on the latest elementary education in Japan. Group meetings will be held in the afternoon, and Chen Heqin will be appointed chairman of the early childhood education group, Ge Liting will be appointed chairman of the lower grade group, and Ma Ketan will be appointed chairman of the middle and upper grade group. A general meeting will be held on the morning of the 11th, and sightseeing will be held in the afternoon. In addition to members, onlookers are welcome. Local Communications

Songjiang 49

Complete Elementary School Graduation Examination The Education Bureau held the county's complete elementary school graduation examination on the 9th. The examination place was in the county high school with a total of 400 students from 18 schools. The examination subjects were Chinese, arithmetic, general knowledge, and English. It was divided into nine sections from 8:00 am to 3:00 pm, supervised by bureau staff. The grading will be announced on the 11th. It is reported that those who pass the examination can be admitted to the county normal school and are exempt from the entrance examination and half a year of tuition. Those who pass the B grade are exempt from the examination to encourage them.

Fourth Anniversary of the Northern Expedition Oath The Propaganda Department of the County Rectification Committee convened representatives from various agencies at the County Party Headquarters auditorium at 9:00 am on the 9th to commemorate the fourth anniversary of the National Revolutionary Army oath. More than 50 representatives from all walks of life attended. Chairman Wu Tianren reported on the significance of the commemoration, the struggle of the National Revolutionary Army, and the direction of future efforts. Then, County Magistrate Jin Qingzhang and Lao Rui, the representative of the Smuggling Suppression Office, gave speeches, and slogans were shouted before the meeting adjourned.

Confessions of Bandit Gu Guilong, etc. Bandit Gu Guilong of Fengjing was escorted to the county yesterday for interrogation, along with a minor bandit named Xiao Pixiu. Du Cheng, the interrogator, opened the court at 9:00 pm and interrogated Gu. The bandit's confession was very impressive. He admitted to the riot, arson, and murder. He was appointed as the pseudo-captain and the fundraising director, and kidnapping for ransom was used as a means of fundraising. He did not know how many people were kidnapped, and he could not remember how many people were killed. Then, the interrogating official summoned the family members of the victims to testify. Some pointed to Gu for killing their brothers, and some pointed to Gu for killing their father and wife. He nodded silently, his demeanor self-possessed. Next, Sun Youtang, or Xiao Pixiu, was interrogated. He admitted to more than 20 kidnappings. The official then sentenced them to be shackled and imprisoned pending review, and forbade the bandits from seeing their relatives.

Fengxian 50

The Lu Kidnapping Case Solved in Shanghai A farmer named Lu Caigen, deceased, from the western half of the sixteenth map of Henan, Zhuangxing, had his nine-year-old posthumous son Zihe kidnapped. The ransom price was reduced from 20,000 to 5,000 yuan. It is reported that the bandits sent another letter two days ago threatening to tear up the ticket if the ransom was not paid in two days. Therefore, Lu's mother and her nephew went to Shanghai as scheduled yesterday to negotiate with the bandits. While they were discussing the ransom price, a member of the Zhabei Security Corps of the Shanghai Special City, surnamed Mao (from Shaoxing, formerly a security official in Zhuangxing), came to Zhuang to report that two unknown men and women had rented a front building ten days ago and acted very secretively, especially monitoring the child, which raised suspicion. Yesterday morning (7th), they took the opportunity to inquire about the child, who initially claimed to be surnamed Chen. After further investigation, he revealed that he was from the Lu family in Zhuangxing. At the same time, newspapers carried similar reports of the kidnapping of the Lu child in Zhuangxing. Fearing a misunderstanding, they came to inquire. Yang Xingsheng, the leader of the second patrol of the Zhuang garrison, verified the previous situation and found it to be accurate. Therefore, he consulted with Lu Ziyun, the clan leader of the Lu family, Shi Jinxiang, the local security guard, and led two squad leaders to Shanghai by boat last night. It is reported that the patrol leader sent someone back to report that Yang and others arrived in Shanghai this morning (8th). First, the plaintiff Lu Ziyun and the contact Mao went to a Mao's house in the American Concession of Zhabei. They looked at the bandit den on the upper floor and saw the kidnapped son being accompanied by a bandit woman. The patrol leader Yang immediately wrote a report in the name of the plaintiff Lu Ziyun and his close relatives Chen Boyi and the local security guard Shi Jinxiang, requesting the local police station to arrest them. At the same time, Mao went to the Security Corps headquarters and went to the place by car with the police station at 8:30 to surround the place. The two male and female bandits had not yet gotten up and were all captured. The Lu hostage was also rescued by Lu Ziyun, who went with them, at the risk of his life. The remaining accomplices confessed that they were living in the Jiangsu Hotel at 117 Wuma Road for the purpose of negotiating the ransom. The police station, fearing that they would escape upon hearing the news, immediately sent four people by car to

The hotel and arrested the gang leader surnamed Fang, who has been transferred to the central police station for transfer to the temporary court for interrogation.

Suzhou 51

Bandits from Hengjing Township Kidnap Villagers Yesterday morning (9th), more than a dozen bandits from Siqian Village, Hengjing Township, entered the county on two boats, each armed with rifles, and rushed to the home of villager Zhu Xiangbao to rob them. Before leaving, they kidnapped Zhu Xiangbao, his wife Zhang, and his daughter Xiao Yatou, three people, and fled west to Taihu Lake.

Bandit Ship Discovered in Maoqi Port Yesterday morning (9th) at about 4:00 am, more than a dozen bandit ships with hundreds of bandits suddenly arrived at Laofentang and Sanguantang in Maoqi Port, Xukou, in the county. Upon hearing the news, the second and third patrols of the County Police Third Squadron rushed to pursue them. The bandits fled towards Wujiang upon hearing the news.

Wuxi 52

Failure to Mediate Labor Dispute in Silk Factories: The labor and management of local silk factories have been in dispute over a contract for a long time, and neither side is willing to compromise, leading to extreme positions. Zhang Hentian, the Standing Committee Member of the County Party Headquarters and the Civil Training Committee, convened a meeting of both parties yesterday afternoon to mediate. It is understood that the Silk Factory Trade Association (the employer side) failed to nominate representatives due to the insufficient number of attendees at repeated meetings. They specially reported the above situation to Zhang, the Standing Committee Member of the Civil Training Committee, who declared that this was the reason why yesterday's mediation failed and needed to be postponed for resolution.

City Property Management Committee Finalized: After the Wuxi Municipal Preparatory Office was ordered to be abolished, a City Property Management Committee was organized to manage the city-owned funds and properties. The committee consists of seven members, with the County Magistrate and the Director of the Finance Bureau as ex-officio members. The other five members are selected by the county from local public figures, with double the number of candidates submitted to the Civil Affairs Department for approval, so that they can be appointed by the county. It is now known that Hu, the Director of the Civil Affairs Department, has approved Qian Sunqing, Yang Hanxi, Li Tiping, Chen Zhanru, and Cai Jiansan as members of the Wuxi City Property Management Committee. Yesterday, a special order was issued to County Magistrate Sun to organize the committee and elect a chairman. County Magistrate Sun immediately sent letters to the committee members, inviting them to take office and scheduling the first meeting at the county government at 2:00 PM on the 14th of this month to discuss all related matters.

County Chamber of Commerce Urges Donations for Price Stabilization: The Xiyi County Chamber of Commerce convened a meeting of representatives from twenty-odd industries, including money, silk, yarn, rice, silk, milling, pawnshops, dyeing, and weaving, at 4:00 PM yesterday to discuss and solicit donations for price stabilization. After a report by Chairman Chen Zhanru, each industry signed up for donations, totaling over 7,000 yuan. To make up the shortfall, another meeting will be convened on the 11th with industries that did not attend to solicit donations and uphold good deeds.

Rugao 53

Rampant Banditry in the Western Suburbs: At midnight on the 4th, during a heavy rain, eight or nine people suddenly sought shelter from the rain at several houses near Wu Sandagezi's place, west of the West Gate's parade ground. After the rain stopped, they took out concealed weapons, tied up Wu Sandagezi and five neighbors. In Guayuan, two miles from the city, a man named Wu San was robbed by a dozen bandits on the night of the 5th, who took his belongings and kidnapped his son-in-law. In Cuijiayuan, near the suburbs, Zhang Guangyu had previously been forced by bandits to pay 200 yuan. Yesterday, more than twenty bandits came again, and the family members escaped through the back door. The bandits then looted all his grain and took his housekeeper. Also, at Cao Changsong's house, four miles from the city, more than ten bandits came after the heavy rain on the night of the 5th, kidnapped Cao's youngest grandson, and went to Cao's widow's house, kidnapping her ten-year-old orphaned son and his nephew.

Informant Also Killed by Bandits: Xie Yuangfu, a farmer from Xiejia Garden in Motou, had previously served the bandits by running errands. Last night, while taking money home from the Zhou family who had been kidnapped, he was suddenly attacked and killed by several bandits with four knife wounds. Also, Zhang Qi, an habitual bandit from Zhangjiadai in the same city, was shot and killed by fellow bandits from Jiang'an Township in front of Zhujiazhuang.

Nantong 54

Banditry Rampant at the Border of Tong and Rugao: The counties of Nantong, Rugao, and Haimen are adjacent. Recently, bandits have gathered and formed gangs. In addition to arson and disturbances, they have even searched houses, collected and burned land deeds, and forced farmers to join the pseudo-Red Army. Any slight resistance is met with tragedy. Li Changjiang, the Jiangbei Bandit Suppression Commander, arrived in Tong from Shanghai and specially telegraphed for the Tai Province police force stationed in Taizhou to concentrate in Tongyi to suppress the bandits.

Various Districts Report Locust Plague: For days, large numbers of locusts have been flying into Nantong from the southeast, with the most severe damage in Qi'an, Shigang, Jinsha, and other districts. Rice, corn, and reed leaves are devoured wherever they pass, leaving nothing behind. Tangzha has been plagued by locusts, and when they fly, they cover the sky. The county government has received reports from various districts and, in addition to working with locust control personnel to eliminate the locusts, has also telegraphed the Agriculture and Mining Department to send personnel to Tong to assist in the work.

Pinghu 55

Xintan Prepares to Launch Price Stabilization: The Xintan District Office, the Public Security Bureau, and the District Property Committee, in order to prevent the occurrence of famine riots in various places, convened a meeting of rice industry representatives and wealthy households at 2:00 PM on the 4th to discuss price stabilization measures. It was decided that District Chief Xia, Public Security Bureau Chief Wang, District Property Committee Representative Yu Shaonong, Xinxianli Representative Cao Dixian, and Shicheng Temple Representative would be appointed, and Gao Xiaolan and others would be hired to form a price stabilization committee, with the City God Temple as the price stabilization location.

Farmers Also Kidnapped by Bandits: Cai Arong, a farmer in Hengmatou with meager assets, was kidnapped by bandits on the 4th and his whereabouts are unknown. His family is very anxious and is now sending people out to investigate.

Lake Bandit Accomplice Cai Arong Arrested: The 2nd Battalion of the 7th Regiment of the Provincial Security Force stationed in this city received a telegram from the Xincang Public Security Sub-bureau a few days ago that there were more than 50 bandits in the Quan Gongting area. Battalion Commander Zhao immediately dispatched soldiers led by Yuan Geng from the 4th company to suppress them. Upon arriving at Quan Gongting, they saw many people wearing straw hats and white clothes in the teahouse. When they saw the troops arrive, they panicked and fled. The soldiers immediately pursued them and captured bandit leader Cai Arong on the spot. The rest escaped by swimming. They also fired shots from across the bank in an attempt to rescue him. Seeing the unfavorable situation, the soldiers divided up and surrounded them. The bandits, unable to resist, scattered and fled. The soldiers and others then captured four suspicious individuals, including Tang Zhaohe, nearby. They were released on bail after the village committee explained and vouched for them. However, Cai Arong, the bandit leader, was the company commander of Taibao Ashu and was confirmed by various villages in Xincang and Luchuan as an important member of the bandit gang. Therefore, he was escorted to Hangzhou overnight yesterday. After interrogation by the 7th Regiment Commander, he was immediately sent to the Security Office for interrogation.

Ding Site's House Robbed by Bandits: Ding Site, a farmer living about two miles from Yaqian Town, was well-off and had long been coveted by bandits. On the night of the 7th, more than twenty bandits armed with rifles and iron rods stormed into his house. Ding Site was awakened from his sleep and, unable to escape, was tied up and tortured by the bandits, suffering severe injuries. They looted more than 100 silver dollars and gold jewelry, worth about 600-700 gold in total, before leaving with a whoop.

Jiashan 56

Tianwang Security Corps Guns Robbed: On the night of the 7th, around 11:00 PM, about fifty bandits speaking with a Tianjin accent suddenly came to Tianning Village and robbed the Security Corps of their guns. The police officers of the Public Security Bureau and three employees of a butcher shop and bamboo shop were shot and injured by the bandits. Jiang Zhebo, the owner of Jiang Santai South-North Goods Shop, and his son, as well as Xue Shushan and four others, were kidnapped by the bandits.

Public Security Bureau Chief Arrives in Shan to Take Office:颜嗣渊 Yan Siyuan, the Chief of the County Public Security Bureau, assumed office on the 8th after being appointed. In addition, Wu Jinming, the Chief of the Fengjing South City Public Security Sub-bureau, was placed under investigation after the case was taken up. The county sent a substitute to take over the case. Ye Zhengzhang, a graduate of the police academy appointed by the Provincial Department, arrived in Shan on the 8th and transferred to Fengjing to take up his new post.

Xiaoshan 57

Detective Kills Policeman While Playing with Gun: Zhu Xueqi, a detective from the Xiaoshan County Detective Team, accidentally shot and killed a nearby policeman on the morning of the 7th while cleaning his gun. The incident was immediately reported to the Public Security Bureau by a nearby policeman, and the detective was arrested and sent to the county for legal action.

County Government Recovers Local Property Funds: The Great Temple in Linpu Town, Xiaoshan, has more than 3,000 yuan in property income from its houses. Although this public fund is jointly owned by the two counties of Shao and Xiao, it has been embezzled by one or two local gentry under the guise of safekeeping. The Xiaoshan County Government learned that this local public fund could be used for local public welfare. It ordered the Fourth District Chief to investigate and verify the matter. If the custodian is found to have embezzled the funds, the safekeeping will be revoked and the funds will be recovered.

Shangyu 58

Fan Shoukang and Others Expected to Be Released Soon: Fan Shoukang, the principal of Chunhui Middle School, and others, who were kidnapped on the evening of the 15th of last month, sent letters to their families from the bandits on the 23rd of the same month. Subsequently, the Director of General Affairs, Zhang Wen, negotiated with the bandits. It is said that the bandits' demands are very high, initially asking for 1.5 million yuan. Later, a fellow villager entrusted a certain magnate to investigate the location of the bandits' lair. After repeated negotiations, the ransom has now been reduced to 6,000 yuan, and it is rumored that they will be released soon. The issue of the continued operation of Chunhui Middle School will also be resolved soon.

The Municipal Government had previously sent letters to the Yin County Party Headquarters and the Yin County District Court to send personnel to supervise the bidding. Bloodshed Over Rice on the Niuzhuang Steamer: More than ten people, including Dong Yin Fuxian, the manager of the Taihe Rice Store, Du Lindi, the manager of the Qiantai Rice Store, and Lou Afu, the manager of the Xieshun Rice Store, were unloading rice on the Niuzhuang Steamer at the Taikoo Wharf in Jiangbei at 3:00 PM yesterday (the 7th). Lou Afu wanted to put the rice leaking from the broken bags back into the original bags, but Yan Sisi, the cargo hold manager of the steamer, refused, leading to an argument that escalated into a fight. At one point, Dong Yin Fuxian and Du Beidi from the rice store side, and Chen Huichun, You Asisi, Yao Afa, and Chen Shirenen from the cargo hold side, all joined the melee, using wooden sticks and iron hammers as weapons. The steamer's comprador, Lin Chuan, rushed to mediate, but only managed to separate them after many people had been injured. They went to the Taikoo Foreign Company to reason, and the rice store side felt dissatisfied. They reported the incident to the First Branch of the Second District Police Station, which took all the witnesses to the station for questioning. After unsuccessful persuasion, the station transferred all the people involved in the case, as well as the weapons such as wooden sticks and iron tools, to the court for review.

Education News

Sports

The Cause and Effect of This Expedition 61

Li Huitang, Captain of the Chinese Expeditionary Football Team

"How can I get 100,000 strings of coins to try leading a team to Europe?" Isn't this the hopeful phrase in my Southern Expedition diary last year? Time flies, and in the blink of an eye, another year has passed. Although I haven't been fortunate enough to get 100,000 strings of coins this year, the fantasy of conquering Europe has now become a reality. Not only has the European trip achieved its goal, but it has also expanded. Our itinerary this time also includes Canada and the United States, making it a round-the-world feat.

I've had the worst luck for the past month. From the National Games to the Da Yun, my body, which has always been fond of movement, has been bedridden for more than two months by the ruthless disease demon. Recovering from the illness and then adding foot troubles has prevented me from participating in both the National and Far East Games. Being sick all the time makes me feel extremely ashamed and resentful of fate. Fortunately, everything has recovered recently, but my laziness is several times greater than usual when my spirit has not recovered and my vitality is still weak, especially when I pick up a pen, I always feel that it weighs thousands of pounds. However, the news about this expedition has awakened my lazy muscles. I feel that there are slight discrepancies in the recent reports, especially in the commentary, which contains counter-propaganda and has a destructive effect. At a time when our drums are beating and our army is about to set off, instead of receiving support and encouragement from all walks of life, we are subjected to this kind of undesirable reaction, which makes me feel at a loss. Like a bone stuck in my throat, I can't bear it. Before leaving Hong Kong, I want to tell all walks of life the cause and effect of the expedition.

My trip south this time is actually entirely for personal matters and has no official business or special responsibility. Since there is no special responsibility, there is no talk of success or failure. The disruptors are only intensifying their work, exaggerating the failure of so-and-so, deceiving themselves and others, and causing the incompetent to disturb themselves, which really makes me laugh.

The motivation for conquering Europe dates back to three years ago, but in recent years it has been troubled by various obstacles. Li Silian, a famous referee in Shanghai, returned to the country on leave last year, and took the opportunity to revive the old proposal, and after half a year of preparation, everything gradually fell into place. The dream of the past will soon be staged from illusion to reality. Before I talk about other things, there are three things to be explained here.

(1) Name: The name of this expeditionary force has caused a great problem. People outside suspect that we are easily crowned with the name Lehua because everything is initiated and organized by Lehua. In fact, why do we have such a meaning? However, it is not possible to contact the other party without a formal organization. As for the name of the expedition, we have already decided to use "Chinese Expeditionary Football Team" ChineseAmatureSoccerTeam, because Lehua's scope is narrow and not applicable. We are not so foolish as to abandon the broad and take the narrow.

(2) Amateur and Salaried: This qualification issue has also been the subject of a very important study, but as far as I know now, the players' future income, such as clothing expenses, daily expenses, etc., are all allowed by the amateur world, and the biggest guarantee is that when the team returns home in the future, the accounts of the entire team will be approved by the accountants of the English Football Association. I remember that before and after the Australian Expedition in 1927, there were also unscrupulous elements who wanted to sabotage and add the crime of being salaried to the team members, but the result was a complete failure. The treatment of the members this time is slightly different from that of the Australian Expedition, and the suspicion of being employed does not need to be overemphasized by enthusiastic people.

(3) Java Tour: A few days ago, counter-propagandists said that this expeditionary force is extremely dangerous. You see, their funding is not secured and they still have to raise funds in Southeast Asia. This kind of argument is extremely ridiculous. There are two reasons why we first travel to Java: (1) Because of Lehua's excellent performance in the Southern Expedition last year, the overseas Chinese specifically asked us to revisit it by the way. (2) Because the European season has not yet arrived, we can take this opportunity to practice in Southeast Asia first to study the cooperation of our team. Planning ahead can be called wisdom. Counter-propagandist, you are too nervous.

After the explanation, I want to talk about the benefits and purposes of this expedition.

Whenever a football team goes on an expedition to a foreign land, in addition to gaining the practical benefits of visiting scenery and expanding their knowledge, the most important thing is to promote the country and improve their skills. The failure of our country's government diplomacy in recent years is not something that needs to be translated. Although our sports are also inferior and thousands of miles behind, anyone will agree that the effect of sports representatives going abroad to promote the country is faster and more effective than that of diplomats and great writers. The seeds planted by the two Australian expeditions are now blooming with brilliant flowers and fruits. This time, the team will travel all over Europe and even to Canada and the United States, which will surely refresh foreigners, especially people from small countries, about the psychology of China. As for improving art, it is the first task of the football world in our country today. Just imagine that the achievements of the Chinese in Hong Kong and Shanghai in recent years can be said to be very outstanding, but the recent Far East Games were evenly divided with the Japanese, who are behind us. Although it is said that there are many reasons why we cannot win completely this time, we are stopping the boat in the middle of the stream, staying in the country and sticking to the old ways. Not only is the progress slow, but there is also a danger of not being allowed to retreat. This expedition to countries with excellent skills and many changes during the competition will definitely absorb the strengths of others. It is impossible to calculate the benefits of their future return to the country to instill them.

There is also the question of how to obtain these talents, which is what all walks of life want to know urgently. Our goal is of course to find the most outstanding members, but there are often various unimaginable difficulties that lead to results that do not live up to the original wish. In my personal opinion, if there is nothing too difficult, in order to achieve both public and private benefits, it is worth sacrificing to what extent to join the team. As for the associations, in order to help each other and cultivate talents for the country, they should also look far ahead and try to send as many skilled players as possible to participate so that they can serve the country and benefit the future of the football world when they return to the country. As far as I know now, there are indeed two or three Hong Kong stars who cannot go with us. Recently, the organizers have had to seek the next best thing because, in order to maintain our credibility, we cannot postpone this matter any longer. If we cannot do it with our hands, we will seek the next best thing. If the next best thing cannot be done, we will seek the next best thing, and even if no one responds at all, Zhao Da and Sun Er will almost have to make up a team. The reason is that our purpose is to go abroad to acquire new knowledge, not like the isolated and angry Sheng Riqian said that we must win to be glorious. Moreover, talking about winning or losing loses the true meaning of sports. Therefore, the complete list of the expedition is not complete until we have found good players in Southeast Asia and are about to depart from Singapore. However, judging from the strength of the players who are currently with the team, at the very least, we can give foreigners a good performance and make them satisfied.

Finally, I sincerely hope that we can gain the deepest practical benefits from this expedition, and that it will not disappoint everyone's sacrifices. On the one hand, I sincerely hope that the sports world in the country can learn from the stimulation of this Far East failure, and that they will no longer observe things through a magnifying glass, but should work through a long-range lens to sweep away the evil winds of self-interest for individuals and associations. Everyone should join hands to improve China and seek the future happiness of the sports world. Please, the journey is imminent, and we will talk about it next time.

Written in Kowloon Inn, 1927.

Results of Yesterday's Singles Handball Competition 62

▲ Sun Daosheng Wins Group A Final

▲ Lu Aibai Wins Group B Final

▲ Cheng Zhenhua Wins Group C Final

▲ Finals for Groups A, B, and C Simultaneously Tomorrow

The All-Shanghai Chinese Handball Singles Competition, hosted by the YMCA, has aroused the interest of the general public. The number of spectators has been increasing day by day, and latercomers have no place to stand. The semi-finals of Groups A, B, and C yesterday were full of wonderful performances. At this critical moment, those who participated were all excited and hoped to win the right to participate in the finals. As a result, Sun Daosheng in Group A, Lu Aibai in Group B, and Cheng Zhenhua in Group C won the victories and jumped into the final scene, competing for the championship with Hong Yuqiu, Hong Rulin, and Luo Shunda respectively. The referees were Zhu Kuan and Gu Yongzhao, and the record keeper was Chen Fuzhang.

▲ Sun Daosheng Defeats Ni Hongen (Group A): Ni's fame soared after defeating the famous general Huang Kesu. Sun, who is known for his experience, did not dare to underestimate the enemy. After the start, Sun's serves were high and fast, making them difficult to return. Sometimes, when the returns were successful, they felt weak and powerless. Sun took advantage of this to launch a killer move and succeeded. Thus, Sun took the lead with a score of 8-2. Ni then increased his score slightly, but the difference between the scores of the two sides was still far. As a result, Sun won the first game with a score of 21-9. In the second game, the two sides were closely matched and it was difficult to distinguish between them. Although Sun's ball skills were better, he lacked energy, so before the score of 11, Ni was able to maintain his balance. Afterwards, Ni plummeted and was unable to defend himself. Sun did not give up and finally won the second game with a score of 21-12, winning the right to participate in the Group A final.

▲ Lu Aibai Defeats Wei Guanghan (Group B): Lu's victory over Wei and winning the right to participate in the Group B final was due to Wei's own fault. In the first game, Lu won with a score of 21-2 with his agile figure and quick hands. It was reasonable. In the second game, the old general Wei was so angry that he used all kinds of tricks to make Lu exhausted. Wei had 20 points while Lu only had 15 points. However, Wei could not get the last point. Seeing Lu's progress step by step, he finally won the second game with a score of 22. If each side had won one game at that time, the outcome of the third game would have been different.

▲ Cheng Zhenhua Defeats Lu Mengsheng (Group C): Cheng's hopes were extremely high in the Group C championship. His skills were so good that he could have achieved good results even if he had participated in Group B. Now he has condescended to Group C, and he should be able to dominate for a while. Yesterday, in the first game, Lu Mengsheng gave Cheng a series of fierce attacks. As a result, Cheng won with a score of 21-15, but he had exhausted his energy. In the second game, Cheng suspended his hands, moving them left and right, high and low, as he pleased. As a result, he won again with a score of 21-10 and won the right to participate in the Group C final.

Private High School Graduates 67

Methods for University Entrance Preliminary Examinations 68

The Ministry of Education has stipulated methods for university entrance preliminary examinations for graduates of unregistered private senior high schools. In addition to a public notice, a telegram was sent via express mail to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities stating that a considerable number of private senior high schools or equivalent institutions in various regions have not yet been approved for registration, and the number of their graduates is also substantial. The Ministry has now specially stipulated these preliminary examination methods for these graduates and issued a public notice for general information. A copy of Public Notice No. 13 is hereby issued, along with the principles of the preliminary examination regulations, instructing the relevant "departments" and "bureaus" to immediately comply with the instructions, formulate examination regulations, conduct examinations, and report the implementation details to the Ministry of Education. (With the official seal of Geng) Enclosed are Public Notice No. 13 and the principles of the preliminary examination regulations for graduates of unregistered private senior high schools, as follows:

▲ Ministry of Education Public Notice No. 13

It has been clearly stipulated by the Ministry that the enrollment of new students by public and registered private colleges and universities shall be limited to graduates of public or registered private senior high schools or equivalent institutions. However, recent investigations have revealed that a considerable number of private senior high schools in various regions have not yet been approved for registration, and the number of their graduates is also substantial. While it is true that many of these students are academically poor and difficult to cultivate, there are also those who are academically excellent and comparable to graduates of public or registered private senior high schools. If strict measures are taken to uniformly deny them the opportunity to further their education, it would seem that these students would be deprived of the opportunity for advanced studies, which is not in line with the fundamental purpose of the state and education in nurturing talent. Therefore, the Ministry has now specially stipulated methods for the admission of graduates of unregistered private senior high schools or equivalent institutions. First, the education authorities of each province and city shall conduct examinations, and those who pass shall be issued a certificate of admission to universities, allowing them to apply to public or registered private colleges and universities. Those who fail shall be given a certificate of transfer to a lower grade, according to their academic level. These preliminary university entrance examinations for graduates of unregistered senior high schools shall be limited to those taking place before August 31st of this year. The examination methods shall be formulated by the Ministry in accordance with the principles outlined below, and the education authorities of each province and city shall be instructed to comply with these principles and formulate their own regulations based on local conditions, in order to facilitate implementation. This is hereby announced.

▲ Principles of the Preliminary Examination Regulations for Graduates of Unregistered Private Senior High Schools

(1) An examination committee shall be established, consisting of one chairperson and six to ten members.

(2) The head of the provincial or municipal education authority shall be the ex officio chairperson. The members shall be appointed or employed by the provincial or municipal education authority from among current education administrators and current principals and teachers of public or registered private high schools or higher institutions. However, the number of administrative personnel shall not exceed one-third of the number of principals and teachers.

(3) The examination subjects shall be based on the curriculum of public senior high schools or equivalent institutions.

(4) The examination shall be held in the location of the provincial or municipal government.

(5) Those who pass the examination shall be issued a certificate of admission to universities. Those who fail shall be given a certificate of transfer to a lower grade, according to their academic level.

The aforementioned certificate of admission to universities shall state that "This certificate is for university admission purposes only and shall not be used for proving other qualifications." The same applies to the certificate of transfer.

(6) Graduates of vocational schools that accept junior high school graduates and provide three years of education shall be allowed to register for the examination.

Ministry of People's Livelihood and Ministry of Agriculture

The Jiangsu Provincial People's Education Institute and the Labor-Agriculture College, in order to improve the methods of implementing social education and promote its smooth implementation, are holding a summer school for social education within four weeks from the 11th of this month to the 9th of August. [>County People's Education

Regulations of the Experimental Zone Preparatory Committee 69

The Shanghai County Education Bureau plans to establish a people's education experimental zone and has begun to implement the plan. This newspaper has already reported on the situation. It is now known that the bureau has organized a preparatory committee for the purpose of having dedicated staff so as to expedite the realization. The regulations of the committee are as follows: Article 1: This committee is named the Shanghai County People's Education Experimental Zone Preparatory Committee. Article 2: The purpose of this committee is to prepare for the Shanghai County People's Education Experimental Zone so that all ongoing matters can be perfected. Article 3: This committee is organized by committee members. Article 4: The members of this committee, in addition to the director of the County Education Bureau, the director of the Social Education Section, the school inspectors, and the education committee members of the school district to which the zone belongs, are ex officio members. Also, the director will invite the district head of the district to which the zone belongs, local gentry, one graduate of the first session of the People's Education Institute, two students of the second session, experts, and

one person to form it. Article 5: The powers of this committee are as follows: (1) To find and decide on the location of the zone. (2) To find and decide on the location of the temporary office. (3) To handle the procedures for using the office building. (4) To discuss and decide on the undertakings to be carried out first during the trial period (limited to people's schools, teahouses, and libraries). (5) To arrange the setting of the temporary office. (6) To discuss the items to be purchased and the equipment to be available for the office and the undertaking. (7) The powers of this committee shall end at the end of the trial period. Article 6: A quorum of two-thirds of the members is required for a formal meeting. Article 7: The meeting period is not fixed and will be convened by the director when necessary. Article 8: The director shall chair the meeting. Local News

July 9th Memorial Meeting 72

▲ Fourth Anniversary of the National Revolutionary Army's Oath to the Northern Expedition

Yesterday was the fourth anniversary of the National Revolutionary Army's oath to the Northern Expedition on July 9th. The Propaganda Department of the Shanghai Special City Party Headquarters held a memorial meeting in the auditorium of the City Party Headquarters at 9:00 am. Representatives from various institutions, organizations, and party departments at all levels in the city were notified in advance to attend the meeting. It is estimated that more than 800 representatives attended. Chairman Chen Dezheng reported on the understanding and efforts that should be made in commemorating July 9th. After that, he shouted slogans and announced the adjournment of the meeting. The details are recorded as follows:

Actively Preparing

National Likin Abolition Conference 73

▲ Jia Shiyi and Zhang Fuyun Both Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday to Assist

▲ Application to the Central Government for Approval of Special Consumption Names

▲ The Issue of Personnel Collecting Taxes in Various Provinces to be Proposed Separately for Discussion

The National Likin Abolition Conference is scheduled to be held in Shanghai on August 15th. Four preparatory meetings have been convened successively, and representatives and proposals from various provinces have been sent or telegraphed en route. Li Hongji, who is in charge of the Likin abolition, believes that with only one month remaining until the conference, the preparation and organization of various matters cannot be delayed. He specially telegraphed Jia Shiyi, Director of the Tax Division of the Ministry of Finance, and Zhang Fuyun, Director of the Customs Administration, urging them to come to Shanghai to assist in the handling of the matter so that they can take office as soon as possible and avoid postponing the conference. Jia and others received the telegram and arrived in Shanghai from Beijing yesterday. According to financial circles, whether the national tax replacement after the implementation of Likin abolition will follow the 1928 Five Provinces Likin Abolition Conference plan and be named Special Consumption Tax has not yet been decided and is still awaiting deliberation at the conference for submission to the Central Government for approval. As for the rate of extraction based on the types and value of goods, due to frequent disasters and poor harvests this year, the conference will consider the local conditions and the price and quality of goods, and even within luxury goods, will determine several levels and decide on the high or low ad valorem tax rate, which must also adapt to the social conditions in various places to avoid the disadvantages of excess. In addition, the issue of personnel from the collection agencies of various provinces will be raised separately for discussion at this conference and will be strictly rectified, it is said.

Article 2 This committee will first set up the following groups and may add more if necessary (A) Management Group (B) Personnel Group (C) Financial Management Group (D) Accounting Group (E) Administrative Group (F) Factory Affairs Group (G) Sales Group (H) Design Group Article 3 Each group of this committee will have one research director and several committee members appointed by the board of directors from among the members. Article 7 These articles of association will be implemented from the date of the board of directors' decision.

Chinese Telephone Users Strive for Sovereignty 76

▲ Telegram to the Central Government

Yesterday, the Chinese Users Association of the Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Telephone Company telegraphed the Central Party Headquarters in Nanjing, the National Government, and the Ministry of Interior of the National Government: We have investigated that the telephone and telegraph industry in our country is clearly stipulated to be state-owned. However, this time, the International Telephone and Telegraph Corporation purchased the assets of the Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Telephone Company without the approval of our government and disregarded our national sovereignty by not obtaining an exclusive franchise from our government. Although our government has repeatedly protested and the public has opposed it, the company has ignored it and acted recklessly. The members of the association are users of the Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Telephone Company and feel it is their duty to not remain silent. Therefore, on June 27, the Chinese Users Association of the Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Telephone Company was established, and Li Zuyu, Hua Huizhong, Zhu Yinjiang, Cheng Zhusun, Tao Leqin, Jin Runxiang, Wang Zhiwei, Hu Fengxiang, and Zhang Yichen were publicly elected as temporary directors. The association's address is No. 4 Shanghai Hong Kong Road. It is determined that the Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Telephone Company is poorly managed. If our government does not actively find a way to recover and operate it independently, it will not be enough to protect national rights and safeguard the interests of merchants and civilians. The association will lead Chinese users to take effective measures and absolutely not cooperate with the International Telephone and Telegraph Corporation as a backing. We hereby telegram to report and request instructions. Another telegram was sent to the Ministry of Communications with the same general idea. Another telegram was sent to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs requesting a serious protest. The rest were also roughly the same and are omitted.

City Chamber of Commerce

Submission of Opinions on Protecting Commerce 79

▲ Submitting a Petition for the National Government to Implement

Since the Municipal Chamber of Commerce took over various documents from the Commercial Consolidation Association, it has been handling each item according to the review of proposals from various industries during the Delegates' Assembly. Here, we select and record important cases as follows:

㈠ Regarding the case of not arbitrarily occupying guild houses without the permission of the industry, a document was submitted to the National Government's Bureau of Social Affairs, the Municipal Party Department, and the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, earnestly requesting protection. The document stated: "Submitting a petition for the resolution of the Members' Delegates Assembly regarding industry guilds' houses, requesting government authorities to strictly prohibit any agency from arbitrarily occupying them without the guild's permission, in order to protect property rights. We respectfully request your review and implementation." This case was brought up on June 21st when the Shanghai Commercial Consolidation Association convened a Members' Delegates Assembly. Representatives from the silk and dried goods industries proposed that guild houses should not be arbitrarily occupied without permission. The original reason for the proposal stated: "Upon investigation, guild houses are often forcibly occupied by labor unions or recruitment committees without the guild's permission. Each industry guild has a tax obligation to the country, and the country should legally be responsible for fully protecting property rights. It is proposed that the Assembly petition the central and municipal party, political, and military authorities to strictly prohibit illegal occupation of houses without the guild's permission, in order to protect property rights," and it was resolved to be handled by the Executive Committee. After the Association was established, it conducted a detailed review and found that the claim in the original case, that labor unions and recruiters arbitrarily occupied guild houses, was a pain commonly felt by each guild. As examples, the houses of the shoe industry guild have been occupied by labor unions and have not been vacated to this day, greatly hindering the Fu Lü Hospital attached to the guild. The Yunshan Elementary School attached to the coal industry guild was occupied by a teacher-led recruitment committee, causing the school to be unable to hold classes. There are many other similar situations too numerous to mention. It is believed that Articles 765 and 767 of the Civil Code's Property Law provide very detailed regulations for the protection of ownership. If any agency can freely occupy property and public power does not stop it, then the law is no more than a written document, and property rights lose their protection. The resulting abuses will inevitably lead to social order being destroyed. Since this case has been approved by the Assembly, it should be recorded and submitted to your office for review. It is humbly requested that you order each labor union and each unit to obtain the consent of each industry guild beforehand and sign a contract approved by a higher authority before moving in if they have no choice but to borrow the houses of various industry guilds in the future. If there is no such procedure, it is clear evidence of one party's free occupation. After each guild reports it, in addition to immediately ordering them to move out, they should also be severely punished according to the circumstances, in order to reverse the trend and provide protection. This is a public benefit."

㈠ Regarding the case of personnel serving in party and government agencies using domestic goods, a document was submitted to the National Government, stating: "Submitting a petition for the resolution of the Delegates' Assembly that party, government, and military agencies have often failed to implement orders to use domestic goods, proposing that the National Government reiterate its sincere admonishment to serve as a warning. We respectfully request your review and implementation." This case was brought up on June 21st when the Shanghai Commercial Consolidation Association convened a Members' Delegates Assembly. According to a temporary proposal by silk industry representative Wu Xingcha, the party, government, and military agencies should comply with the National Government's order to use domestic goods. It was resolved to be approved. After the Association was established, it was transferred by the Commercial Consolidation Association. It is believed that the regulations on clothing have long been stipulated, and all materials should use domestic goods. Furthermore, your government has issued clear orders and sincere admonitions regarding the promotion of domestic goods, which should have led to a rapid transformation and subtle influence, so that domestic silk and satin would have the hope of being revived. However, after examining the actual situation, not only are domestic silk, cotton, and other products unable to reverse the trend, but they are also gradually declining and closing down one after another, to the point that they are almost unable to sustain themselves. The general public tends to follow the fashion, regarding imported goods as trendy and domestic products as shabby. And the senior officials of party, government, and military agencies, who have the responsibility of leading the public to change customs, have also failed to avoid this trend. As a result, the public is also being influenced and assimilated. This kind of frenzy will lead to hundreds of millions of farmers and workers being displaced, shaking the foundation of the country. Is the danger not small? Wei Wen Gong's cloth garments in ancient history have been praised as a beautiful story, which is sufficient to show that promoting thrift and plugging loopholes is a common principle of ancient and modern times for emerging countries. To reverse ingrained habits, it is especially important for those who have the responsibility of setting an example for the people to be able to lead by example, so that the general public will not laugh at the mention of promoting domestic goods, viewing it as a fashionable formality. This is what is meant by teaching by example. It is hereby submitted to your office for review. It is humbly requested that you reiterate your admonishment to all party, government, and military agency personnel that all clothing must be made of domestic materials. Those who disobey should be subject to reputational sanctions by the leaders of their respective agencies, so that the declining trend can be reversed and domestic production can be revived. We are eagerly awaiting orders."

Leased Location of the Resident Office in Shanghai 80

In order to facilitate contact with China, the International Labour Bureau has specially dispatched Secretary Chen Zongcheng to China to establish a branch in Nanjing and appointed Mr. Chen as the director of the bureau. Compensation from Shanghai Arsenal to be Paid Out 81

The Shanghai Arsenal previously had an accident in the drug-loading room, resulting in the death and injury of more than 30 workers. The arsenal has submitted two requests to the headquarters and the Ministry of Military Administration for compensation for the bereaved families. In addition to a temporary allocation of 120 yuan for funeral expenses, it also requested 500 yuan per person for compensation. The headquarters subsequently approved only 300 yuan per person. The compensation will be paid out next Monday (i.e., the 13th). However, the arsenal believes that the drug-loading workers have been working in the factory for 20 to 30 years, and no better compensation can encourage newcomers. Therefore, it has taken out another 2,000 yuan from the arsenal's public surplus funds and raised more than 1,600 yuan from employees, expecting that each of the deceased can receive a total of 500 yuan. As for the injured, the amount of compensation will depend on the severity of the injury, generally at least 15 yuan for minor injuries and up to 150 yuan for serious injuries. Yesterday, the arsenal has sent letters to each family member, informing them to collect the money from the factory on time. The accident of the drug-loading workers in the arsenal, which has been delayed for more than a month, can be completely resolved next week.

The Association of Families of the May 30th Incident Will Be Delayed 82

The Association of Families of Martyrs of the Shanghai May 30th Massacre originally scheduled to end its work after June 30th. Now, due to the newly registered injured comrades Wang Ruping, Li Yixun, Mei Zhonglin, Zhou Renlian, Wei Chunting, Liu Shaoxian, and Chen Yunqiu, who were registered by a lawyer, totaling eight or nine people, the Association of Families is actively conducting separate investigations and verifications. In addition to the two representatives Hu and Chen, the Association has only two staff members, Secretary Zhou Zaisheng and Clerk Sun Guangfu. With few people and many affairs, they are unable to complete the work in a short time. It is estimated that the two procedures of investigation and verification can be completed in the next week, and the fifth batch of condolences can be paid out at the beginning of the next week. After this batch of condolences is paid out, the winding-up work will begin. It is also learned that the Association has hired accountant Jiang Xinzhao as an accounting consultant to check all condolence payments and other accounts on its behalf, and will publicly report on them.

News of the Strike by Workers at the French Concession Water and Electricity Company Yesterday 83

The various sections of the conciliation meeting held by the workers of the French Concession Water and Electricity Company have already been recorded in previous reports. Here, we explore and record the situation yesterday as follows:

▲ Foremen were discovered at the meeting. The workers' union held a meeting of 600 workers in the stadium on the day before yesterday. Suddenly, more than a dozen foremen were found to be attending the meeting (foremen are not workers and are not members of the union). They intended to represent the workers to contact the factory to negotiate conditions and solicit the opinions of the workers. However, all the workers believed that this action was a running dog of the capitalists and unanimously rejected it. Therefore, the foremen came with enthusiasm and returned with disappointment. ▲ Each labor union decided to help the union. Representatives were sent to contact each labor union to request assistance and report the facts about the French factory's unreasonable oppression and deception. It is said that each level of labor union was filled with righteous indignation. As soon as the meeting is held for discussion, the method of assistance will be announced.

▲ The Municipal Party Department, which is deeply worried about the delay in resolving the strike by the French electricity workers, will convene a meeting with party, government, and military representatives this afternoon to discuss countermeasures.

▲ A petition may be filed today. At 9:00 a.m. today, more than 600 workers of the union will go to the Municipal People's Training Association to petition. A Case of Dispute in the Western Clothing Union 84

▲ Firing Workers Without Reason

▲ Causing Major Negotiations

Five people from Ningbo, including Zhou Baomo, Tu Xinggen, Zheng Youshui, Shao Kaihuai, and Hu Akang, have been working as tailors in the fire brigade of the Public Concession on Wusong Road in this city for four years and have been getting along well. However, for some unknown reason a month ago, the fire brigade suddenly ordered the dismissal of the five workers, causing major negotiations. According to the investigation, the Western Clothing Union in this city immediately contacted the fire brigade in writing and also sent a letter to request the Public Concession Chinese Ratepayers Association to help urge the Industry Bureau to give preferential treatment to the workers. Because the fire brigade refused to yield, all the requests of the union were rejected. Although the Chinese Ratepayers Association claimed to have sent a request, the Industry Bureau has not made any response for many days. Therefore, the executive committee of the Western Clothing Union is holding joint meetings every day to discuss this case. It is said that it has drafted five concrete measures: ㈠ Send a letter to urge the Public Concession Chinese Ratepayers Association to urge the Industry Bureau to reply as soon as possible; ㈡ Submit a petition to the Municipal Party Department and the Bureau of Social Affairs to take charge and convene a labor-capital arbitration committee to resolve the issue when necessary; ㈢ Advertise to all labor unions in the city to request unanimous support to facilitate negotiations; ㈣ (Omitted); ㈤ Call on all Western clothing workers to march and demonstrate and petition the fire brigade and the Industry Bureau of the Public Concession until a satisfactory solution is reached.

Increased Passenger and Freight on the Beiyang Class Sea Liner 86

Since the issue occurred at the Tianjin Customs, the import and export of passengers and goods have been greatly reduced. Some of the commercial ships of various countries have temporarily suspended sailing, and some have changed their routes. In recent days, because the Ministry of Finance has properly arranged the method for the Shanghai Customs to collect taxes on its behalf, the transportation of passengers and goods has returned to its former state. In recent days, the number of passengers and goods on each sea liner sailing from Shanghai to Tianjin has suddenly increased. The Shengjing Maru, which exported yesterday, carried more than 1,000 tons of various goods, including about 10,000 bundles of paper and about 1,200 bags of sugar. Other sea liners of British companies Jardine Matheson and Butterfield & Swire also carried many goods. In addition, the Tangshan Maru, which sailed from Tianjin to Shanghai yesterday, also carried more than 1,000 tons of passengers and goods. The transportation of goods between Tianjin and Shanghai has returned to its original state.

Navigation News from the Upper Reaches of the Yangtze River 87

▲ Shashi Can Pass Through In the past week, bandits similar to the Red Spear Society were discovered along the Yangtze River from Shishou and Gong'an in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River to the Shashi area, obstructing merchant ships sailing up and down the river. Subsequently, Britain, Japan, and the United States each sent one or two warships to escort them. Yesterday, the Shanghai shipping companies received a telegram from Hankou stating that the bandits had been defeated by the army and that it was safe to sail up and down the Yangtze River from the 8th. Export goods from Shanghai to Shashi and other ports can now be loaded.

▲ The Japanese Wheel Maintains the Status Quo After the sharp drop in silver prices, the upstream shipping of Nissin Steamship Company has been affected by the increased expenditure on ships and has not been able to increase the water fare without authorization. Last month, the president of the company came to China from the east to inspect the ports along the Yangtze River and advocated reducing the number of shifts on the Changde, Xianghu, and Yanghe lines above Hankou to save expenses. This matter has been resolved, but recently, the company, in view of the fact that the Chinese and British shipping companies in the Yangtze River line are increasing ships and expanding, has temporarily changed its plan to cancel the contraction plan of reducing ships and shifts and maintain the status quo.

▲ The Wanliu Can Be Rescued The Swire Shipping Company's Wanliu Wheel ran aground 40 miles downstream of Chongqing, the hull was damaged, and the engine was also damaged. Now, a telegram from Yichang said that after the cargo in each cabin was unloaded, the hole was being repaired and temporarily coated with cement to make it float to the surface of the river. The project will be completed soon and can be towed to Shanghai for major repairs.

The Iceberg Maru's Maiden Voyage Arrived in Shanghai 88

▲ Sailed to Hong Kong Last Night

The new sea liner Iceberg Maru, built by Nippon Yusen Kaisha for the Americas and Asia, arrived in Shanghai on its maiden voyage from Japan the day before yesterday at 9:00 p.m. It was berthed at the Huishan Wharf. Yesterday afternoon, Chinese and foreign guests were invited to visit. The hull is strong, the equipment is luxurious, and the engine is particularly new. Therefore, the speed of travel is higher than any ocean liner currently in service. It has a deadweight of 11,600 tons, and the cabins are graded and all use the latest scientific equipment, which is extremely luxurious. At about 7:00 p.m. it set sail for Hong Kong.

Then, Shen Nianxian gave a speech on the organizational law of the cooperative, Zhang Hanyun, a representative of the Municipal Propaganda Department, gave a speech on the significance of the cooperative movement, and Lu Rensheng gave a speech on the relationship between the cooperative movement and the livelihood of the people. Then, there was a performance. Qiujiang Elementary School's dance included four sections: ㈠ Little Swallows, ㈡ Falling Flowers and Flowing Water, ㈢ Su Wu Herding Sheep, ㈣ Picking Water Chestnuts. The postures were beautiful and the singing was very pleasant, especially Ms. Zhou Lindi's (5) Jiangsheng team's comedy (Thief Catching Thief) (Laughing Play) was slippery and funny (6) The Labor University graduates' boxing skills (7) The Public Security Bureau's Beijing opera were all very pleasant to listen to. The meeting ended at seven o'clock. In terms of propaganda, in addition to the propaganda teams from the seven districts, five or six kinds of cooperative propaganda materials were distributed, which were very popular with the public.
