Some People Advocate Imposing a Western Clothing Tax 90

▲ Wu Chao Gong's Letter to Wang Yansong

Since the Executive Committee of this city resolved to strictly prohibit party and government personnel from wearing Western clothing and recommended Wang Yansong to consult with the municipal government on handling the matter, Wang Yansong drafted a plan and sent a letter to the French Municipal Government for discussion. Now, Wu Chao Gong, a citizen living in Si Da Li, North Sichuan Road, advocates levying a Western clothing tax to incorporate the prohibition in the collection. He sent a letter to Wang Yansong yesterday. The original letter said: (Omitted above) The Municipal Party Department discussed and strictly prohibited party and government personnel from wearing Western clothing at the 22nd meeting and recommended Mr. Wang to consult with the municipal government on handling the matter. Gong is very happy that the proposer has the same heart as me and hopes that the proposal will be passed and implemented. Upon investigation, the goods imported by our country over the years are more than the exports, of which clothing items account for the majority of the imported goods. Because Chinese people regard foreigners as the supreme superiors and regard themselves as inferior and despicable, they must wear Western clothing, eat Western food, and live in Western houses. There is no need to say that the daily necessities are all fashionable from foreign countries and regard domestic products as敝屣 (discarded like old shoes). Initially, it was due to the compradors and servants of foreign firms, followed by students who imitated them, and then businessmen and even unemployed idlers who wore Western clothing as superiors. Now, there are more than a hundred times more people wearing Western clothing in Shanghai than a few years ago. If this continues for more than ten years, all people in Shanghai, from the intellectual class to the rickshaw pullers, must wear Western clothing. If the government still turns a blind eye and does not take action, I am afraid that in a few years, no one will ask about Chinese cotton cloth and silk, silver will flow out, the people will be poor and their wealth will be exhausted, there will be more unemployed people, and there will be more bandits. Recalling a few months ago, the Silk Association used all their efforts to create various advertisements to persuade Chinese people to remove Western clothing and use domestic goods. However, the speaker was sincere and the listener was indifferent and there was no effect. The intellectual middle class is willing to be a foreign slave and has no patriotism. It is difficult to achieve practical results if this kind of slavery is admonished with good words, and there is no way to do it without coercive measures. Moreover, the people in the inland areas follow the dress in Shanghai, so Shanghai can be called the model district for clothing in the country. If Shanghai does not strictly take action, it will be even more harmful to follow it in the future. Therefore, it is better to levy a Western clothing tax than to persuade them to remove Western clothing. All Chinese people who want to wear Western clothing must go to the government office to pay the Western clothing tax, charging 50 to 100 yuan per person per year. In this way, if the prohibition is incorporated into the collection, there will naturally be fewer people wearing Western clothing, and the accessories of foreign goods will also be reduced accordingly. Then domestic goods can be promoted without mentioning it, the factory will be developed, and the unemployed can also be slightly less. If only party and government personnel are banned, it will inevitably be a incomplete measure and the effect will be small. Gong Xue is ignorant and has little knowledge to help the times, but I have fulfilled my responsibilities as a citizen and dare to make humble opinions in order to seek your guidance. I only ask that you, sir, go further and teach me. I am extremely apprehensive and panicky.

▲ Salvaging the Sunken Ship After the Diepputot number, a coal carrier of the 开濼 (kai po) Company, was sunk by the Japanese ship Fengtian Maru, the 开濼 company began planning yesterday for how to deal with the aftermath. The Haizhu Bay where the accident occurred is within the Beiyang shipping route, which all ships must pass through. If it is left unsalvaged, it will hinder the traffic of the waterway and endanger the ships. Therefore, it has contacted the Shanghai manager of the Tokyo Salvage Company of Japan to discuss the salvage procedure. It has now been agreed that it will begin salvaging after the shipowner Johnson returns to Shanghai and asks about the situation.

The company has already made representations to Dalian Steamboat Company. The two companies have decided to ask an impartial person to investigate the truth and then submit it to arbitration for public judgment. As for the Fengtian Maru, a telegram has been sent to Shanghai saying that the slight damage to the bow has been repaired and it will be allowed to sail to Shanghai on the 12th.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce LP]

Please Exempt the Export Tax on Ground Sugar 92

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Finance yesterday, saying that the Sugar Trade Association previously wrote a letter stating that the customs and tax department considered it to be a local product and ordered it to pay the export tax again if they purchase and transport Javanese sugar, grind it into fine sand and sell it, which they could not afford, so they requested that it be forwarded for cancellation. The former Commercial Consolidation Association believed that Javanese sugar was imported by Dutch ships and had already paid the import tax in accordance with regulations. According to the usual practice of foreign goods, not only is the original piece packed and shipped, but also disassembled into parts, and it has never been taxed repeatedly. The reason is that although the packaging is different, the quality and composition have not changed, so it cannot be strongly pointed out that it is a local product transformed from foreign goods. The industry grinds Javanese sugar to suit the market, but the characteristics and taste remain the same, and the composition has not changed. As cited in the original letter, the imported pigments and butter are disassembled and mixed, and the Fat Tian powder exported by Bu Neimen is mixed with impurities, but they are not taxed as local goods. However, for the ground Javanese sugar, which does not change the original quality, it is ordered to pay the export tax separately as a local product, which is inevitable to make Chinese merchants feel short of breath. Moreover, it is said that the commission earned on each load of ground sugar is only a few cents, but the export tax is ordered to be 45 cents per load, so no sugar merchant is willing to lose money to operate this trade, which is tantamount to vigorously opening up sales channels for Japanese sugar. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce was telegraphed to review and request cancellation, and on May 28, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce approved the cancellation of the telegram and informed the Ministry of Finance to review and handle the matter. It is respectfully known that the telegram was ordered to be investigated and handled. On June 21, when the former Commercial Consolidation Association convened a meeting of members and representatives of various industries to establish the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Sugar Trade Association again submitted the previous situation and applied for relief. It was resolved to transfer it to our association for handling at the second executive meeting of our association on July 7. According to the previous case, we respectfully requested your department to seek the Lord. It is hereby recorded and presented for your review. It is telegraphed to request that you quickly investigate and handle it. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce requested that the method of repeatedly taxing the item of ground Javanese grain by analogy with the transformation of local goods should be cancelled, so as to maintain the business of sugar merchants and serve the public. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce respectfully kowtows.

Luo Xishun Requests Investigation into False Accusations 93

The Labor Union of the Pharmaceutical Industry yesterday submitted a document to the Citizen Training Council and the Social Bureau of the City, stating that the petition was made to refute malicious accusations and maintain a livelihood and reputation. It was reported that the union had received a letter from member Luo Xishun stating that he had recently read a news item in the local newspaper about Xi Changsheng's dismissal of employees and how difficult things were. He was shocked that the employer dared to fabricate such accusations under the clear blue sky, spewing venomous blood to harm people, and that the intention was so sinister that it was infuriating. The previous time, he fabricated accusations and presented them to the Municipal Social Bureau. Fortunately, the Social Bureau saw through his tricks and ordered him to reinstate the worker, but Xishun had already suffered a lot of mental pain. However, the employer was still not satisfied and falsely accused him to the trade association by fabricating facts. The shop owner, Xi Shaofeng, was inherently impatient, irritable, and unreasonable. Three years ago, he suddenly suffered from a mental disorder, which occurred and healed from time to time, several times a year. Now, he is using this to falsely accuse him, which is ridiculous. It is very common for shop employees to join or leave, so how can it cause the shop owner to have a mental disorder? Even if there is a possibility of inducing illness, the shop owner has been ill for three years, and Xishun joined the shop last fall, which are all facts. Judging from the principles of things and human feelings, discerning people can easily judge the right and wrong without Xishun's detailed defense. However, since he has used such insidious tricks, he has to report all the facts to the union so that it can handle the matter impartially. Since Xishun has been serving in the shop, he has been clean and self-respecting, cautious and devoted to his duties, and has never dared to be negligent. However, he is inherently honest and straightforward, and flattery is not his forte. The shop owner's wife has the deepest dictatorial ideas, and she does not understand the work situation of the shop employees at all. She interferes at every turn, and if things do not go as she wishes, she scolds endlessly. The other employees dare to be angry but dare not speak out. Only Xishun, for the sake of his own personality, cannot help but stand up and question when there is too much oppression. Therefore, the shop owner's wife's hatred is even deeper, which is a major reason for her repeated thoughts of falsely accusing him. Just like the previous false accusations to the Social Bureau, fortunately, the matter was resolved impartially and it was decided to reinstate him. The shop owner actually said in the petition that the dismissal failed because the union was protecting him. Does he regard the laws and regulations of the Social Bureau as worthless? He is reversing right and wrong to such an extent. However, the shop owner, Xi Shaofeng, is known for his violent nature. The shop owner's wife (the second wife) is even more tyrannical and unreasonable. Conflicts often arise between the husband and wife, leading to a mental disorder.

This is an undeniable fact. Unexpectedly, the shop owner's wife used this to falsely accuse Xishun. The ignorance of a woman is not enough to blame deeply, but unexpectedly, the trade association also does not understand the truth and does not ask for the truth. It rashly distributed the slanderous petition to the newspapers, deliberately destroying Xishun's reputation and the future of the workers, which is very dangerous. Xishun is only concerned with the livelihood of his whole family and endures humiliation and begs for help. The shop owner actually thinks that the weak can be bullied. He falsely accused the worker Gu Mingxing last fall, but now he falsely accuses Xishun, how can Xishun endure it? Therefore, he has specially written a document requesting the union to forward it to the higher authorities to appeal for injustice and to request the shop owner to compensate for the loss of reputation in order to warn the mischievous. The union has approved this and sent personnel to investigate, and it was reported that the accusations made by the shop owner's wife were completely fabricated and had no evidence. According to this, it is specially requested that the union (bureau) impartially criticize and approve appropriate punishment to warn the mischievous, maintain a livelihood, and protect reputation. This is the most convenient way. (Omitted below) It is heard that the employee Luo

Xishun has directly sent a letter to the National Pharmaceutical Industry Association, demanding a clear reply within three days and will resort to law to file a claim for damages to his reputation.

Salary Issues for Railway Employees 94

The salaries of employees of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways have always been based on monthly salaries. Those with monthly salaries above one hundred yuan receive an annual salary increase of ten yuan per month, and those with monthly salaries above fifty yuan receive an annual salary increase of eight yuan per month. This time, the Ministry of Railways promulgated a salary scale in which those with monthly salaries above fifty yuan receive an annual salary increase of only five yuan per month, and the highest salary for section members is only one hundred and eighty yuan. All employees believe that the current prices have increased several times, but the fixed salaries are less than before, and the salary increase of only five yuan for those with more than fifty yuan is not enough to cope with the environment and maintain life. Many employees of the accounting department have submitted a request to Director Liu to consider the special circumstances of Shanghai and approve the request to the Ministry of Railways for special treatment, and to continue to follow the old rules.

A Young Hardware Store Owner Extorted for 300 Yuan 99

▲ Rescued on Meixie Road in Nanshi

▲ Three Male and Female Kidnappers Arrested

Song Ruisheng, the five-year-old son of Song Runsheng, the owner of Runchang Hardware Store at 181 Datong Road, Zhabei, disappeared while playing at the door at about 9:00 am the day before yesterday (the 7th). Unexpectedly, the kidnappers sent a letter that afternoon, demanding 300 yuan to redeem him. Song knew that his son had been kidnapped. The next day, he received another letter and reported it to the Fourth District General Administration, which immediately ordered detectives to make two arrests. This morning, they broke the case in Hexinli, Meixie Road, Nanshi, rescued the hostage, and arrested the kidnappers Chen Xiaoyun and others. The details of the case are as follows:

▲ Family Store, Song Ruisheng, a 30-year-old man from Pudong, runs Runchang Hardware Store. It is a single storefront business that is not bad, but the economy is not wealthy enough. His wife, Tao, 32 years old, has a daughter, Gendi, 8 years old, and a young son, Yunfu, 5 years old, who are not in school. Song is quite frugal. There is only one employee in the store, who is responsible for managing accounts and other matters, while his wife and daughter assist in the store's business, making it a family store.

▲ Young Son Disappears, At around 9:00 am on the 7th, Song's young son, Yunfu, was playing in front of the store when a man suddenly offered him candy and gave him a few copper coins. Yunfu, without knowing anything, fell into his trap and followed him happily. At first, Song did not think much about it. When it was time for lunch and he still had not returned, he became suspicious and sent out detectives, but there was no news. His wife cried bitterly.

▲ Two Letters from Kidnappers, While Song and his wife were full of worry and at a loss, a letter was delivered by the post office. After opening it, it turned out to be a ransom letter from a kidnapper. It said, "Brothers,

We have been unemployed for a long time and are in economic difficulties. We are borrowing 300 yuan. Please wrap the money in white paper and put it in garbage can number 125 next to Shenxiutang on Xinzha Road at 3:00 am. We will send someone to pick it up. Do not be stingy or you will regret it." It was signed Xu Yongchang. After receiving the letter, Song was shocked and didn't know what to do because he didn't have such a large sum of money. He decided to ignore it. Unexpectedly, he received another letter the next day with harsh words, saying that if he didn't find a way to redeem the ticket, it would be unfavorable to his whole family. The contact point was in Peideli, Xinzha Road. The person who came must hold a newspaper. Song reported to the Fourth District General Administration for investigation because the time was tight.

▲ Enemy Mastermind, After receiving the report, Director Jin immediately ordered his subordinates to cooperate with Team Leader He Xiong, Detective Zhou Guicai, Li Guiqing, Yao Ziyun, Shi Yunling, Zhao Zhennan, Li Zongnian, and others from the Detective Team to secretly go to the address together with the detectives from the Xinzha Police Station, disguised as beggars, villagers, and vendors. Unexpectedly, after waiting until 3:00 am yesterday, no one came. Detective He had an idea and questioned Song about whether he had any enemies. Song suddenly remembered that Chen Xiaoyun, whom he had known recently, had come to his house to ask about the kidnapping of his son, which was suspicious. Detective He went to 48 Nanxing Road, Zhabei, and arrested Chen. After a strict interrogation, Chen confessed that he was the principal offender and that he had written the threatening letter. The hostage was currently hidden on the front floor of No. 5 Hexinli, Meixie Road, Nanshi.

▲ Rescuing the Hostage, After the detectives learned the location of the hostage, they notified the Second District General Administration in advance at around 9:00 am yesterday and secretly surrounded the neighborhood. They broke into house number 5 in the neighborhood and found the young hostage being held in a woman's arms. They stepped forward, snatched him away, and brought the woman, Chen Yao (22 years old, from Zhenjiang), and the second landlord, Xu Wu (from Shanghai), along with them. Director Jin asked them in detail one by one. He ordered that the principal offender, Chen Xiaoyun (23 years old, from Zhenjiang), Chen Yao, and Xu Wu be sent to the Public Security Bureau for strict handling because the case was related to kidnapping. The hostage, Song Yunfu, was handed over to his family to take back.

A Blind Man's Wife 100

▲ Has Two Lovers

▲ And Both Are Blind

▲ Triangular Blind Love

▲ Almost Caused a Tragedy

Yesterday afternoon at around 6:00 pm, a three-blind-person love affair involving one woman occurred in the jurisdiction of the Second District General Administration of Nanshi. One of them attempted suicide by opium due to unrequited love, almost causing a tragedy. The matter was quite strange. The details are recorded as follows:

▲ A Blind Man Marries a Romantic Woman, Zhang Aliu, a local blind man, 35 years old, currently residing at No. 10 Heshengli, Laoximen, Nanshi, makes a living by chanting scriptures. He married Zhang Zong, a local woman, 34 years old, who is ugly in appearance and naturally flirtatious. Seeing that her husband is blind, she often looks for new love. As a result, scandalous rumors spread far and wide.

▲ Co-conspires with Another Blind Man, Zong knows that she is ugly and knows that it is not appropriate, so she specializes in co-conspiring with blind people. There is a blind fortune teller from Songjiang, Hongkou, named Jin Dehai (37 years old), who is familiar with Zhang. In April of this year, he and Zong had an ambiguous relationship. Although Zhang knew about this, he acted like a fool and a deaf man, implementing the policy of the henpecked husband.

▲ Also Falls in Love with a Third Blind Man, After Jin had an affair with Zong, they had been living in peace. Unexpectedly, before a month had passed, Zong became tired of him again and had an affair with Xu Xingsheng (37 years old, from Wuxi), Jin's uncle, who lived at No. 94 Siheli, Lujiabang. Xu is also blind and works as a fortune teller. Before long, the matter was heard by Jin. Jin was extremely angry, but he was afraid that the matter would be leaked out, which would be unfavorable to both parties, so he kept it a secret.

▲ Xu Xingsheng Actually Hides, Xu Xingsheng, seeing that Zhang Jin'er was obstructing him, could not get what he wanted, so he thought of occupying her for himself. On the 28th day of the previous month, he hid Zong at No. 6 of a technique-based family in Furunli, Xinzha Road. Five days later, Zhang Aliu discovered it and immediately gathered a group of hooligans and snatched Xu and Zong back together on Xinzha Road. It was agreed that Xu would pay 30 yuan.

▲ Losing Both Person and Money, Planning to Suicide, Xu had no money, so he discussed it with Jin, saying that if Jin was willing to pay 30 yuan, the rights would belong to Jin alone. Jin agreed, and the money was handed over to Jin the next day, and he actually lived with her. Unexpectedly, although the matter was over, she still could not forget Xu, so she quarreled with Jin all day long, looking for trouble on purpose. A few days ago, she suddenly disappeared again. Jin, seeing that he had lost both person and money, was ashamed and angry, so he secretly swallowed a full dose of opium last night at 6:00 pm.

▲ Neighbors Noticed and Sent to the Police Station, Fortunately, the neighbors noticed it at that time and urgently reported it to the Sanguantang Police Station of the Second District General Administration. The patrol officer rushed to the scene and sent Jin to Shanghai Hospital. Fortunately, he had not swallowed it for a long time and the poison had not erupted. After the doctor irrigated him, the poison was completely vomited out. He was then sent to the General Administration together with Zong and others. After Director Wang asked a question, Jin confessed that in April of this year, my (I refer to myself) sister gave me more than 100 yuan for my mother's funeral expenses, which were all spent on Zong. Now I think that I have lost both person and money, so I swallowed opium to commit suicide. After Director Wang took the confession, he immediately prepared a document and sent it to the General Bureau for verification.

Dispute over the Mobilization of the Yidu Steamer's Crew 105

The American Shangjiang shallow steamer Yidu, which travels along the Yangtze River in the Yichang area, recently suffered damage to its hull and came to Shanghai to enter the Qiuxin Iron Factory Shipyard for repairs. During this period, a trend of the company mobilizing the entire crew of the steamer occurred. It is estimated that dozens of people have been dismissed, from compradors and accountants to tea attendants and handymen (except for sailors and drivers). The compradores of the steamer did not know it at first. Yesterday, Mr. Zhou, the newly appointed general comprador, brought all the newly appointed crew members and a letter from the company to the captain, requesting to take over the matter. The old crew refused to hand over the matter. At the same time, the old general comprador asked the captain to take 7,000 yuan of deposit cabinet money and 450 yuan of salary, and asked the captain to sign a receipt immediately so that he could claim it from the company. The captain said that the mobilization of the crew was entirely the company's intention and he was absolutely not involved, so he did not agree. The old crew members did not hand over the ship and leave the ship, so the new crew members could not take over, which caused a long brewing. Later, the old crew's big and secondary compradores went to the company to negotiate, but they could not resolve the matter satisfactorily for a while. The captain of the steamer reported to the water patrol police station for investigation because the old crew refused to hand over the ship's affairs, which caused the ship to be stranded. Tan Huang Song was sent to investigate the ship. The old three compradores, Mr. Wang, stated the difficulty of not being able to leave the ship for a while. Tan ordered that all the old crew members on the ship must land before 12:00 noon tomorrow (today) and must not stay away again, and notified the captain to allow them to stay on the ship for one more day and expedite the handover at the same time. The old crew members requested to negotiate with the company. It is estimated that the dispute over the handover of the new and old crew members can be resolved from now on.

How Can Someone Who Doesn't Know How to Swim Swim? 106

▲ Chen Guibao Died in Vain

Chen Guibao, a 21-year-old man from Yangzhou, lived at No. 13 Guixiangli, Linheng Road, Ximen. The day before yesterday afternoon at around 3:00 pm, he suddenly went to the Suzhou River to take off his clothes and swim because the weather was hot. Because he didn't know how to swim, his body sank to the bottom of the river. The spectators on both sides couldn't see him coming up and tried to rescue him in every possible way, but Chen's body drifted away and he couldn't be rescued, so he drowned in the river. The body had not floated up until the evening. Yesterday morning at 6:00 am, Chen Changming, a member of the corpse family, reported to the water patrol police station to pay attention to finding the body for collection. It is said that the deceased was bare-chested and wore a pair of blue cloth pants.

Why Are There So Many Male Corpses in the Pu River? 107

Yesterday morning at 6:00 am, the water patrol police west patrol retrieved an unidentified male corpse wearing a blue cloth shirt and pants on the bank of the Pu River at the Jiujiang Road pier. At 9:00 am, an unidentified male corpse was found on the bank of the Pu River on Renji Road. Both were brought to the police station. In the afternoon at around 2:00 pm, another male corpse floated up in the Pu River at the mouth of the Suzhou River, about 30 years old, wearing a blue cloth shirt and pants. The police station's No. 15 Chinese patrol retrieved the body to the police station. The two male corpses were collected by the Salvation Bureau's patrol ship and the Corpse Transport Bureau, and the corpse family was notified to identify and claim them.

The Jin Chen Divorce Case Was Resolved Amicably 108

Jin Axi from the county hired lawyer Shen Yong to sue his wife Chen Aer in the local court for disturbing and demanding money, requesting a divorce to prevent future troubles. The statement stated that he married the defendant as his wife in August of the Republic of China's sixth year. However, the defendant could not settle down. In the Republic of China's eighth year, the defendant fled without a trace and took his daughter Lin Xian with her. It was learned that the defendant had an affair with someone named Wang in Dachang Town and lived like a couple, giving birth to a nine-year-old son. It was also learned that Lin Xian had been sold. Now the defendant suddenly came to disturb him, but the couple had already broken up and the water was difficult to recover. Moreover, the defendant had recently been smoking opium and there was no possibility of reunion. There were four reasons for divorce: ㈠ When she fled, she took everything with her, even the incense burner, wax poles, and sundries. ㈡ It has been 12 years since she fled and there has been no news, except that she came home once in the Republic of China's eleventh year. ㈢ She sold the plaintiff's daughter Lin Xian without a trace. ㈣ She has been living with Wang Arluan and has a nine-year-old son. He requested permission to grant the divorce. Yesterday, Judge Yang Keqian opened a court hearing. The plaintiff Jin Axi stated the previous situation and questioned the defendant Chen Aer. The defendant completely denied it. The judge reconciled them in court. As a result, the plaintiff paid the defendant 50 yuan and both parties separated. The judge stated that according to the facts, there was no reason to give money, but considering the hardship, a small amount of compensation was given. Both parties expressed their willingness to reach an amicable agreement and signed the papers to leave the court.

Li Xingjuan's Divorce Case

Unable to Summon Her Husband 109

▲ Permission Granted to Arrest and Prosecute at Any Time

Li Xingjuan, a woman from Minhang, is 29 years old this year. She married Wu Baoqing (from Anhui) from the same town ten years ago through a matchmaker. However, Wu liked to wander around and did not engage in production. Therefore, all of Xingjuan's clothes and decorations were pawned shortly after she married. They lived together for three years and gave birth to a son. It was not enough to sit and eat the mountains empty. It was difficult for a clever woman to cook without rice. Forced by hunger and cold, Xingjuan had no choice but to leave home and find a place to eat. She was introduced by someone to work in a hospital and was diligent and thrifty, and was highly regarded by the hosts. She also asked someone to find Wu Baoqing a job, but Wu was lazy and soon lost his job again. With no way to make a living, he often went to Xingjuan to demand money by force. If he did not succeed, he would say rude things. Xingjuan could not bear the burden. For the sake of her lifelong happiness, she had no choice but to divorce him. Therefore, she hired lawyers Wang Zengxian and Yuan Xilian to file a petition with the local court, requesting a judgment to allow the divorce. Yesterday, Judge Du opened a court hearing. The defendant did not attend because his address was unknown and he could not be served. The plaintiff Li Xingjuan stated that she is now working as a nurse at Dr. Gong's place at No. 16 Zhenxingli, Linyin Road, Ximenwai. She married the defendant Wu Baoqing more than ten years ago. Wu is 36 years old this year and is said to still live in Minhang Town. Since she got married, the defendant has had no job and has been gambling all day long, disregarding the use of household items. The plaintiff can only find her own way to make a living. Since they separated, it has been ten years. The defendant occasionally asks the plaintiff for money to squander. Moreover, she has repeatedly recommended him for business, but he stops immediately, which shows that the defendant is bad. Now the plaintiff only earns more than ten yuan a month in salary, and her personal life is often insufficient. Where does she get the extra money to support his waste? She requested permission to divorce. The official asked if you had met the defendant recently. She replied that the defendant had sent a letter this year. At this point, lawyer Yuan stood up and presented the defendant's letter for inspection and said that our lawyer's office is a voluntary organization and does not charge fees. Because the defendant often harasses the plaintiff and cannot be reasoned with, he once advised the plaintiff that divorce is not a good thing and it would be best not to divorce, but the plaintiff insisted on the divorce, so he filed the lawsuit. The interrogator asked the plaintiff again and then stated that the defendant could not be summoned and the judgment could not be made today. Now the lawsuit in this case is suspended. If the plaintiff meets the defendant in the future, she will arrest the defendant and bring him to court for verification. The plaintiff obeyed the argument and retreated.

The Sister Dies and the Younger Sister Succeeds Her 110

▲ The Zhu and Xia Families Reunite Again and Again

Xia Kuitang, a native of Jiading, works in a Shanghai money shop. He has three daughters. The eldest is married and the second daughter, Yizhen, 21 years old, was studying at a school in Suzhou. She graduated last year and is now at home. In February of this year, she was betrothed to the son of the Zhu family, named Xiaohashang, to be his wife. A lucky day has been chosen to marry in November. Unexpectedly, Yizhen suddenly suffered from fever in the middle of last month and died on the 26th of last month. Xiaohashang from the Xia Family Wooden Bridge was extremely anxious when he received the news. Zhu has only this one son to comfort him. It is said that Xia's third daughter is not yet betrothed. After obtaining Xiaohashang's consent, he negotiated with the matchmaker. Xia's second daughter died of illness and his third daughter is not yet betrothed. Now he is willing to marry his third daughter. After the matchmaker told Xia and Xia also obtained the consent of his third daughter, the matchmaker told Xiaohashang, who was very happy. His father is now choosing a lucky day to get married and is returning the previous Geng Tie to the Kun residence.

A Pair of Shameless Sister Flowers 111

▲ Shi Wanzhu Teases and Laughs Proudly

Su Hongxi, a native of Xinghua, who lives at No. 27 Wujia Street, Machine Factory Street, Nanshi, is a rickshaw puller. His wife, Zhang, is 22 years old. She is not bad in appearance but is inherently lewd. Shi Wanzhu, a 22-year-old man from Taizhou, is also a rickshaw puller and lives with Su. Seeing that Zhang is quite beautiful, he tried to seduce her and soon fell in love. Su knew about it but endured it without saying anything. Zhang has a younger sister who is of age and often comes to her sister's house to play. The day before yesterday, the sister came again. It happened that Su was out for business. At around 11:00 pm, Su returned home. When he wanted to enter the room, he suddenly heard laughter coming from inside the room. He felt strange and peeked through the crack in the door. He saw his sister-in-law naked and bare, bathing in the bathtub. Shi was also teasing and performing all kinds of strange actions. Su was filled with jealousy when he saw it and became very angry. He immediately pushed the door open and twisted Shi. A big conflict arose. His sister-in-law jumped out of the bathtub, put on her clothes, and slipped away. The matter was heard by Zhang Wanxiang, a guard on duty at the 19th post. He rushed to the scene and brought the men and women to the first branch of the first district. After preliminary interrogation by the director, he ordered the men and women to be detained temporarily to await verification because they were both shameless.

Yellow Ferry Woman Accuses Adoptive Parents of Restricting Freedom 112

A twenty-one-year-old woman from Huangdu, Zhou Amei, was adopted by Shen Xiaomei as her adoptive daughter at the age of five. Shen remarried Li Shiqin after her husband passed away, and brought Zhou to Li's house. When Zhou was twelve, Li and Shen sent her to work at the No. 4 Cotton Factory for Internal and External Affairs. All her wages were taken by Li and others. Once, Zhou asked Li and others to buy her clothes because she lacked clothing, but was instead severely beaten. Li and others had originally planned to marry Zhou off to someone with the surname Wu in Wusong on the 19th of last month. Zhou only found out about this a few days prior and was very unwilling. Two days before the wedding date, Zhou secretly went out and hired a lawyer to draft a complaint against Li and Shen in the Special District Local Court, accusing them of restricting her freedom and requesting that they be punished according to Article 318 of the criminal law. The case will soon be opened for trial by the court.

Xia Yunfeng and His Wife Agree to Divorce

Xia Yunfeng, a native of Ningbo, married Zhu Meili, a fellow villager, eight years ago. They have since had two children, a boy and a girl, but the boy died young, leaving only their four-year-old daughter, Meimei. Recently, Zhu has been increasingly concerned about Xia's growing opium addiction, which has led him to neglect the support of his wife and children. Forcibly Abducting a Prostitute and Extorting Money 113

Yesterday, Guan Chen, the madam of the Rui'an Lane No. 13, Aligre Road, French Concession, a brothel for young prostitutes, filed a complaint with the Criminal Court of the French Court, stating that her establishment’s prostitute, Chen Ruifang, was forcibly abducted by a group of armed men last month. The next day, the defendant, Liu Fubao, sent someone to invite the madam to have tea at the Yile Tian Teahouse. He said that if she wanted the prostitute back, she would have to pay a reward of four hundred yuan before she could be released. At that time, the madam agreed to pay three hundred yuan, and the defendant agreed to hand over the person in seven days. Unexpectedly, the handover was repeatedly delayed. Therefore, she reported the matter and requested the arrest of Liu for investigation. Liu Fubao testified that the prostitute was the wife of a civilian friend, Wang Shengcai. He did not know how she was abducted by a gang, and there was no extortion involved. He requested a thorough investigation. The Chinese and Western officials instructed both parties to present their evidence. Liu was released on bail pending further investigation by the police and a subsequent review.
